# Snellio-Ramæum philosophiæ Syntagma, tomis aliquot separatis distinctum; Quibus continentur 1. Generales sincerioris philosophiæ Ramææ informationes : 2. Dialectica, 3. Rhetorica, 4. Arithmetica, 5. Geometria, 6. Sphæra, seu astronomia, 7. Physica, 8. Psychologia, 9. Ethica ; Rhodolphi Snellii, excellentissimi philosophi, commentationibus succinctis & accuratis ; sed cum aliorum huius æui præcellentissimorum viroru[m] lectissimis observationibus ac notis studiose passim collatis & auctis; explicatæ : quibus præfatio D. Rhodolphi Goclenii, celeberrimi in Marpurgensi Academia philosophi, præfixa est.

- 著者: Snellius, Rudolphus
- 初版: 1596
- 情報源: [archive](https://archive.org/details/BIUSante_pharma_res011431x04)
- パブリックドメイン: ✓
